Tree AdministrativeArea (Region)

Get a tree of the Regions with the most important information started from defined Region.

```php
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo 'Exception when calling DefaultApi->webcamWeather: ', $e->getMessage(), PHP_EOL;
}
?>
```
